Deprecated: array_key_exists(): Using array_key_exists() on objects is deprecated. Use isset() or property_exists() instead in phar:///home/lbakken/development/php-amqplib/php-amqplib/phpDocumentor.phar/vendor/twig/twig/lib/Twig/Template.php on line 527

On 64 bit systems it will return always unsigned int value in 0..2^32 range.

On 32 bit systems it will return signed int value in -2^31...+2^31 range.

Use with caution!
